[30;1m416 | [0m[35m.. note::[0m
[30;1m417 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m418 | [0m[35m   Our plugin's ``authenticate`` method does not assume that the keys[0m
[30;1m419 | [0m[35m   ``login`` or ``password`` exist in the identity; although it[0m
[30;1m420 | [0m[35m   requires them to do "real work" it returns None if they are not[0m
[30;1m421 | [0m[35m   present instead of raising an exception.  This is required by the[0m
[30;1m422 | [0m[35m   ``IAuthenticator`` interface specification.[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m251[0m[34m of [0m[33m632[0m[31m ]--[0m
   Rule Id: [34mBD000701[0m
       Tag: [34mSecurity.Backdoor.DataExfiltration.Token[0m

  Filename: [33m/repoze_who-3.1.0/docs/plugins.rst[0m
   Pattern: [32m(npm owner|password|htpasswd|auth_?token|secret_?key|private_?key|authorized_keys?|npmrc|\.ssh|usersecrets?|api_?keys|nuget\.config|\.identityservice)[0m
[30;1m409 | [0m[35m``authenticate`` implementation grabs the login and password out of[0m

[30;1m408 | [0m[35menvironment and an identity.  Our SimpleHTPasswdPlugin[0m
